INC-SOURCE Beam intensity is 1 to 2 uA. (Their uncertainties were E141100100015 
           estimated to be about 5-10%.)                          E141100100016 
SAMPLE     - Chemical-form of target is element.                  E141100100017 
           - Physical-form of target is solid.                    E141100100018 
           - Target-thickness is 0.1 to 0.3 mg/cm2.               E141100100019 
           - Backing is aluminium. Each target was wrapped with a E141100100020 
             sheet of Al thick enough for stopping all fission    E141100100021 
             products.                                            E141100100022 
METHOD     (STTA)                                                 E141100100023 
           (BCINT) The beam currents were typically 1-2 micro-A.  E141100100024 
           (ACTIV) The targets were bombarded for periods of      E141100100025 
                   30-min to 2-hours.                             E141100100026 
FACILITY   (VDGT,2JPNJAE)                                         E141100100027 
           (CYCLO,2JPNTOK) Institute for Nuclear Study            E141100100028 
DETECTOR   (HPGE)                                                 E141100100029 
ADD-RES    (COMP) The weighted mean mass number of the light and  E141100100030 
                  heavy asymmetric peak, the FWHM of the heavier  E141100100031 
                  asymmetric peak, the peak-to-valley ratio.      E141100100032
